Adoration Chapel&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Dearest Jesus, ever present in the most Blessed Sacrament of the Altar, it is good to be here with You.&#160; Thank You for Holy Mass and Communion this morning.&#160; Thank You for waiting patiently for us to come visit You, my Jesus, my King.&#160; I love You!&#160; Lord, I am very surprised to hear about the death of (name withheld).&#160;&#160; How very sad.&#160; Please take his soul to Heaven.&#160; Comfort and console his family and (name withheld).&#160; Help her to begin anew and to draw close to Your Sacred Heart and the Immaculate Heart of Mary.&#160; She must be shocked by this sudden illness and death.&#160; Her dreams and plans completely changed.&#160; Take this time of sadness and make it a time of growth and grace, Lord.&#160; Jesus, You said ‘Behold I make all things new.’&#160; Give her Your heart, Lord.&#160; Give her Your peace.&#160; I pray also for (names withheld).&#160; Help (name withheld) to draw close to You through these illnesses and give (name withheld) strength and patience to walk with her husband in the face of illness.&#160; Lord, there are so many people in need of Your healing.&#160; Please heal (names withheld).&#160; Please guide those who have left the Church, back.&#160; For all who do not know Your love may they realize and believe that You are the Christ, Son of the Living God.&#160; Praise You, Lord.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Thank You for holy priests, Jesus.&#160; Thank You!&#160; Please protect them, Lord.&#160; Purge the sin of evil from within the Church, Lord and bring comfort and healing to the afflicted.&#160; Lord, may the new springtime come soon.&#160; Please bring about the Triumph of the Immaculate Heart of Mary.&#160; Bring all souls to the joy of conversion and healing.&#160; Reunite all Christians, Lord.&#160; Shepherd us, Lord.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Jesus, I was thinking about the deep sadness and concern, the great depth of anxiety, the Blessed Mother and St. Joseph had for You when You were separated from them as a child.&#160; I can’t begin to imagine how distraught they felt as they searched for You among relatives, then pilgrims and all the people in the city of Jerusalem.&#160; What joy they had when You were found teaching in the temple.&#160; Jesus, there is such joy in finding You.&#160; May all who have lost their way in life have great joy in finding You.&#160; Lead them to You, Lord and give them the joy of their lives.&#160; Jesus, help my brothers and sisters to find You, the Light.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“My child, trust in My plan for the world, for those you love, for those who are lost and for the broken hearted.&#160; There are many things that cannot be understood from the vantage point of those living in these times.&#160; They can only be understood in time, with time and by the light all who reach Heaven will receive.&#160; It is meritorious to trust in Me, especially when you do not understand.&#160; My plan is perfect, because it is for love of souls.&#160; You know this, My child because you have come to believe.&#160; Encourage others in this, for it is truth.&#160; I can be trusted with the best possible plan for each soul.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Yes, Lord.&#160; Thank You!&#160; Sometimes we take circuitous routes to You, Lord.&#160; Jesus, there is so much darkness, even in the church now, but it has been dark in previous times and I know You will bring us through this.&#160; I know, because You are holy, perfect, and merciful, Lord.&#160; In Your justice and in Your mercy, You allow mankind to make choices for good or for evil due to the gift of free will.&#160; But, You will not allow evil to continue to the point of eradicating the Faith.&#160; You always have a small remnant somewhere Lord.&#160; I am thinking of the Israelites in captivity in Babylon.&#160; You eventually freed them, Lord, even though they were in captivity because they had turned their backs on You and had rejected You, the One True God!&#160; We have done this as a society, Jesus.&#160; There are many who love and follow You still, so please have mercy on us, Lord though we are sinners.&#160; Help us to find our way out of this mess with the assistance of Your Most Holy Mother Mary.&#160; Jesus, I trust in You.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“My little lamb, you have heard that My Mother is cleaning, purifying, sweeping the dirt and filth and this is true.&#160; All is being perfected and cleansed.&#160; When one cleans house it always looks worse during the process.&#160; Furniture is moved, cleaning supplies are in the middle of the floor, buckets, mops, rags are in sight and everything looks out of place.&#160; This is the way it is when deep cleaning is in progress.&#160; Sometimes it is difficult to see the dust, grime and dirt until it is examined closely.&#160; You have commented before that you didn’t realize how dusty the table was, until the room was filled with sunlight.&#160; This is true of sin, also My little one.&#160; Sinful people do evil under the cover of darkness.&#160; They keep their sins hidden and silence their victims.&#160; Because I am a just Savior, I will not allow evil to continue unnoticed.&#160; It will come under scrutiny by the light of My justice.&#160; Now, My child is the uncovering period.&#160; More evil will be brought out into the light.&#160; It must be so, for the sake of My justice and also My mercy.&#160; Too many innocent victims cry out for justice and justice will be theirs.&#160; The spirit of Judas, the spirit of pride, materialism and greed still tempts those who serve for wrong reasons in My Holy Church.&#160; Pray for these men, My child.&#160; If they do not repent, it will not go well with them.&#160; I have said that those who cause My little ones to sin would be better off had they not been born.&#160; This is a harsh saying, My little one, yet it is true.&#160; Pray for the innocents, but also pray for the perpetrators of such evil for their judgements will be very harsh if they do not repent of their evil acts.&#160; Many lives have been destroyed.&#160; I remind you that I am the great healer of broken hearts and I can deliver victims from these atrocities and raise them to victory.&#160; Pray, pray, pray.&#160; My child, I am with you.&#160; I am with My Church.&#160; The Church will survive just as I have promised, but it will be purified and the cancer must be extricated.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Lord, I pray for cooperation in the hierarchy.&#160; May the leaders, the shepherds cooperate with Your Will and may they stand for holiness, purity and love. Do not allow evil to be swept under the rug, Lord but faced squarely and challenged in the light of Your mercy and truth.&#160; Let us be about the clearing and cleaning to bring about the new springtime.&#160; Help us to get through the time of ‘spring cleaning’, Lord.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“My child, My child, it will come to pass but it will be some time yet for it takes time to purify hearts.&#160; Once My Church is cleansed it will once again be a light to all nations and a place of refuge.&#160; Keep your eyes on Me and ask My Mother to guide you.&#160; Hold fast to Her hands and do not focus on all that is evil, but focus on all that is good.&#160; Be joy to others.&#160; Be joyful followers, My children.&#160; I recognize that you are weary from the many battles.&#160; This is why you must seek frequent refreshment in the Sacraments.&#160; You need the graces, the strength that I alone give.&#160; Draw nearer to Me, My children.&#160; This is not the time to run from Me for I have not committed this evil that you wish to flee.&#160; Flee evil and come to Me, for I am holy, sinless and pure.&#160; I am all love, goodness and mercy.&#160; Do not confuse evil acts of those in the church, with Me, the Good Shepherd.&#160; The Church is holy, but not so with all its members.&#160; This is not as it should be, My little ones, however sin entered into the world in the Garden and has been in the hearts of mankind every since.&#160; This is why I came from Heaven, was born of Mary taking on humanity so that I, the Son of God and the Son of man could redeem you.&#160; You have been redeemed for a great price, My life.&#160; I poured out every drop of My blood for you, My children and at great pain and suffering.&#160; The depth of My physical suffering was nothing compared to the suffering of My Sacred Heart broken for those who would reject Me and choose hell.&#160; I was tempted, My children and this was My greatest temptation, knowing I would die for all but not all would choose salvation.&#160; My children, rejection by the ones I love so deeply was the cause of My greatest suffering.”&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Lord, please help those who reject You today, to repent of their sins and turn to You.&#160; Embrace them, Lord in the arms of their Savior.&#160; If they only knew how beautiful, how merciful, how loving You are they would have no fear.&#160; Jesus, heal them of the fear they may have.&#160; Give them courage and humility to turn to You.&#160; You always forgive when we have contrition.&#160; Give the graces of contrition to those who do not see the magnitude of sin.&#160; Help us all to repent, Jesus for we are all sinners.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“This is a good prayer, My little lamb.&#160; I will always have mercy for those who have strayed from Me, when there is sorrow for sin.&#160; There must be sorrow for sin, though or there will only be judgement.&#160; While souls are alive, there is time for conversion, so do not wait, My lost children.&#160; If you wait, it could be too late.&#160; You do not know the hour when you will take your last breath and come before Me in judgement.&#160; Do not put off for tomorrow what you can do today.&#160; I am the living bread, come down from Heaven.&#160; Come to Me so that you may have eternal life.&#160; My child, My child, the times I have foretold are fast upon you, but you must be steadfast in your faith and firm in your convictions bearing all suffering with love for in this way you and all who sacrifice and suffer for the Church and for souls will gain the victory.&#160; You, My Children of Light bear the light of Christ in your hearts.&#160; Give witness to Me, to the truths of the Faith, the One Holy Catholic and Apostolic Church and in this way, you bring the Good News to the lost and forsaken.&#160; Offer all suffering in penance for the sins of the shepherds who have betrayed and in some cases, harmed the sheep.&#160; Pray for those who persecute My Church.&#160; Remember, when they persecute you they are persecuting Me.&#160; My children, I hear your prayers and the cries of My little ones wounded and betrayed.&#160; I know of your pain, for I was with you when you were harmed.&#160; They harmed Me, also.&#160; I did not stand by as one who witnesses a crime, I was not a bystander.&#160; I was with you and in you.&#160; When you were harmed, I was harmed.&#160; When you were victimized, I was victimized.&#160; Their egregious acts were not done in isolation, though that was their intent.&#160; Sin is never done in secret for I am with those who are harmed.&#160; I am also harmed.&#160; You do not understand this, but it is truth, for I am one with you, My children.&#160; This is the meaning of the passages in the Gospel that whatever you do to the least of Mine, you do to Me.&#160; It is also true that whatever you fail to do for your brothers, you fail to do for Me.&#160; Examine yourselves, My children, be the light of Scripture.&#160; Repent of all sins and confess so that you will be renewed by grace, forgiven of your sins and part of the family of God once again.&#160; You who have been wounded, I know how very deeply you were wounded.&#160; My little children who suffer much, who are full of pain and perhaps even filled with fear, I your Jesus understand.&#160; I, too have been wounded.&#160; I was scourged, beaten, humiliated in My humanity.&#160; I was naked as they beat Me; wounded for their and others’ transgressions.&#160; I, too was innocent, having never sinned, for I AM the sinless One.&#160; I was mocked, crowned with thorns that penetrated the outer layer of My brain.&#160; When I thought I could bear no more I was forced to carry a heavy cross, though I had no strength to do so.&#160; I willed Myself to carry it, on My bloody shoulders, for love of you.&#160; I walked the stony road to Calvary with you in mind.&#160; I saw you before Me though you had not yet come into existence.&#160; I did this for love of you.&#160; I, too was faced with people not only wanting to kill Me, but who were killing Me and I forgave them.&#160; I did this so that you would see that you must also forgive.&#160; You must forgive, My children wounded and betrayed.&#160; Follow Me and forgive your enemies.&#160; Pray for those who persecuted and persecute you still.&#160; Through forgiveness, you will break free.&#160; Do not allow them to continue to persecute you by your hatred for them.&#160; Free yourselves from this bondage by forgiving them.&#160; They committed horrible atrocities against you, My beloved and yet I ask you to forgive as I forgive.&#160; ‘This is impossible,’ you say?&#160; It may seem impossible right now, but with My help it is possible.&#160; You must do this, for your own sake.&#160; Give your woundedness to Me.&#160; Give Me the terrible memories, the guilt, the shame, the fear.&#160; Give it all to Me.&#160; Allow Me to have this, My beautiful sons and daughters.&#160; Your wounds are safe with Me and Me alone.&#160; I am the great physician, healer, friend.&#160; Allow Me to heal you.&#160;&#160; If you do not think you can forgive at this time, I understand.&#160; All I need is your willingness to try.&#160; In your will, say, ‘Lord, I am unable to forgive these egregious wounds, but I know You command forgiveness of our enemies.&#160; Since I am unable to forgive, You must forgive through Me.&#160; You forgive them, Jesus and teach me to want to forgive.’&#160; Pray this, My children.&#160; This is all I need; your willingness to try.&#160; Your willingness to do My Will, though you are unable at this time.&#160; I will take this open, festering wound, and pour graces for peace, healing and love that you so much deserve and need from your Jesus.&#160; I love you.&#160; You did not deserve to be harmed, My little children of love.&#160; You did not deserve it.&#160; You deserve protection, truth, love, a father and brother who will never let you down, who will never desert you, let alone harm you.&#160; I am this brother, this father.&#160; I will not let you down.&#160; I am with you and in you.&#160; Come, let Me help you to heal and to have victory in your lives.&#160; This does not seem possible, I know.&#160; It did not seem possible to Martha and Mary when I arrived after their brother, Lazarus had been dead three days and was in his tomb.&#160; I raised him from the dead, My children.&#160; You can be resurrected, too.&#160; I am calling to you now, just as I called to Lazarus.&#160; I said, ‘Lazarus, come forth!’&#160; He came to life and immediately heeded My call, even though he could not see due to the cloth wrappings covering his head and his body.&#160; You see, he loved Me and he heard My voice and answered, even from his tomb.&#160; You may feel that you are dead in spirit though your body is alive.&#160; I tell you now, that I can heal you and bring you back to spiritual life and I want to make you whole again.&#160; Only I have the power to do so, but you must do as Lazarus and come forth.&#160; You must come to Me, just as he did.&#160; If you cannot, for you have no strength and you are afraid, then I will send My sweet, pure, tender Mother to you.&#160; She will hold out her kind hands to you.&#160; Take them.&#160; Look in her pure, unspoiled eyes and allow Her to guide you.&#160; She will bring you to My tender, loving arms and you will see all that you are hoping for, all that you need, all that seems too good to be true, you will find in Me, your Jesus.&#160; I love you.&#160; You will be safe with Me.&#160; Come, do not be afraid.&#160; You are safe in My Sacred Heart.&#160; I will make you whole again, but you must come to Me and allow Me to heal you.&#160; Behold, I make all things new.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Thank You, Jesus, my Lord and my God.&#160; Thank You for Your deep love for mankind, for Your children.&#160; Help us, Lord to come to You no matter how much we have been wounded, no matter how broken and bruised.&#160; Comfort the afflicted ones, Lord.&#160; Thank You for Your mercy and Your love.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“My Sacred Heart is wounded for love of My children.&#160; Console Me with your love, My little lamb, My daughter.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;I love You, my Jesus, my Lord, my God, my Savior.&#160; I love Your Sacred, Merciful Heart wounded for our transgressions.&#160; I love You, Most Holy Trinity, Father, Son and Holy Spirit.&#160; I love You in the Most Holy Eucharist, in Your Church and in the poorest of the poor.&#160; Jesus, in Your humility, You become bread to nourish our souls.&#160; Teach me to love You in the Eucharist.&#160; Teach me to love You through the crosses You allow me to carry.&#160; Teach me to love You in my brothers and sisters and in those who persecute me.&#160; Teach me to love and to forgive as You love and forgive.&#160; Give me Your Holy Mother to guide and direct me since She followed You perfectly and loved You more than any other human being could love via Her Immaculate Heart.&#160; Help me to be more loyal and faithful to You than I have before.&#160; I love You, Jesus and I want to love You more.&#160; Saints in Heaven and angels ask Jesus to give me graces to love heroically so that I can be more like my Savior.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“Thank you, My daughter.&#160; I love you.&#160; You are growing in love, My child and I will give you graces for love.&#160; Thank you for your love and friendship.&#160; Go now in My peace.&#160; I bless you in the name of My Father, in My name and in the name of My Holy Spirit.&#160; Go in peace and in My joy.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Amen.&#160; Thank You, Lord.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;wixGuard&quot;&gt;​&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;wixGuard&quot;&gt;​&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;September 2, 2018&#160; Adoration Chapel&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Hello, Jesus ever present in the Most Blessed Sacrament.&#160; It is good to be here with You.&#160; Thank You for Holy Mass this morning and Holy Communion.&#160; Thank You for my family, my fellow parishioners and friends and for the many blessings You give to me which I do not deserve.&#160; You are so kind, generous and merciful.&#160; Praise You, my Lord and my God.&#160; Lord, thank You for Scripture and for the teachings of Holy Mother Church.&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Jesus, please comfort, heal and console all who are ill.&#160; Thank You, Lord for healing (name withheld)!&#160; Praise You, great physician and healer.&#160; Thank You for Your merciful love.&#160; Please help all who are ill especially (names withheld), all who suffer from cancer and Alzheimer’s.&#160; Please heal (name withheld) and restore faith in You to (names withheld) and their families.&#160; Please bring about reconciliation with Your Church all who have left including (names withheld) and all fallen away Christians.&#160; I pray that (names withheld) and all their families will be converted and all non-baptized will come through the waters of Baptism in the Holy Catholic Church.&#160; Cover all those who hope in, believe in, and love You with Your holy mantle of protection.&#160; Bless and protect all who have refuges to provide for people during the Time of Great Trials.&#160; Help us Lord in this hour of great need.&#160; Be with us Lord and keep us close to Your Sacred Heart.&#160; I love You, my Jesus.&#160; Help me to love You even more.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Lord Jesus, have You anything to say to me?&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“Yes.&#160; Please write My daughter.&#160; Today there is little love and very little faith.&#160; Peace in the hearts of mankind has been lost, therefore peace in the homes and in the nations is threatened.&#160; Mankind, busy about many things that are of no consequence, does not notice even family members and friends, let alone strangers.&#160; There is much hustle and bustle as people race from one event to the next from meeting to meeting, concert, to restaurant, work and play, but no time for the Lord God who created the world and mankind.&#160; No time to give thanks for all I have given to each and every person.&#160; There is no time for God and no time for one another.&#160; Even when families are together each person is doing something disconnected from one another.&#160; If they do sit together, the children are hushed so as not to interfere with the entertainment of the moment.&#160; This is not family life, My children, because you are not living, but only existing.&#160; Take the time to talk with one another, to rest, to pray and even to play together with your children.&#160; By doing so, you will be showing respect and care for one another.&#160; When you do your chores around the house, include your children in the work.&#160; Teach them responsibility and respect for the things provided to you by the work of your hands and the blessings of God.&#160; Do not allow your children to be detached from you and from your home.&#160; Do not allow them to think that you, the parents, are their servants.&#160; This is not wise parenting.&#160; Teach them to do things for you and show them your joy that they are doing something to please you. &#160;They will learn to love through work and sacrifice when they make something or do something needed.&#160; Even though young children cannot accomplish the work as you would, it is still worthwhile and good.&#160; Be pleased when they show effort.&#160; Encourage them.&#160; You are showing gratitude and this is how they will grow in virtue and gratitude to you and for God.&#160; Be thoughtful and kind to one another.&#160; Do not put your entertainment first before your relationships.&#160; Live simple lives of work, rest, play, and being together.&#160; This is how the Blessed Mother and Saint Joseph lived and taught Me to live.&#160; St. Joseph taught Me to work when I was very young, by making things for My Beautiful Mother Mary.&#160; Fathers, teach your children how to work.&#160; Start with small, simple chores.&#160; Show them what to do, then praise them when they have completed the task.&#160; Teach them to do things for their mother and in this way, they learn respect and love for their mothers.&#160; Doing small things for one another, being grateful for what they do for you is something basic that everyone can do.&#160; This is a simple step on the path to holiness, My children.&#160; Teach your children to do simple acts of kindness for one another and in this way, they are also showing love for God who made each person in His image and likeness.&#160; This is true for everyone, even My children who are adults.&#160; You may think, ‘This is too simple, Lord.&#160; Surely You aren’t speaking to me?&#160; I already know to be kind.’&#160; To which I say, ‘You may know this, but are you doing something kind and loving each day for someone else?&#160; Are you taking time to speak to those you pass each day as you hurry on your way?&#160; Are you being love to your family members and making your homes a place of simplicity, peacefulness and love?’&#160; You may know this, but I want you to renew your commitment and faithfulness for this is one way of living the Gospel.&#160; My children, I realize that many of My faithful ones do not have the home life, the family, the faith being lived by others, that you desire to have.&#160; You are Mine though and I am yours and therefore you are called to live with this love, the love I give you.&#160; You are called to love the other who does not know love, who does not even act as though they desire love.&#160; You must love them.&#160; You may be the only person on earth who will teach them about My love by giving them love.&#160; They may have hurt you time and again, (I am not referring to physical wounds but emotional disappointments or wounds) but you must forgive and love as I have loved.&#160; Remember, I died for you so that you would have salvation and so that you would know how much I love you.&#160; When others do not show love, show them love and mercy.&#160; Be kind, even when they do not return kindness.&#160; Pray for them, My children.&#160; Pray and forgive.&#160; Be at peace for you have a beautiful Father in Heaven who loves you.&#160; He is with you as I am with you.&#160; Be at peace.&#160; All the love you give to those who do not love you in return, will be showered upon you in Heaven.&#160; You will receive this and so much more.&#160; Do not worry, for I see everything, My children.&#160; I know each kind turn you have done for another, each and every smile, every nice and thoughtful act of service done in private and every prayer.&#160; I know every kind word, every time you listened attentively and with love.&#160; I know how you were received and if you felt unappreciated, know that I appreciate you.&#160; I care for you.&#160; I am interested in all that you have to say and I love you.&#160; Nothing you do out of love is ever wasted.&#160; No sacrifice, no prayer, no act of love, no good thought, nothing, nothing is wasted.&#160; Do all for the love of My children for in this way you do it for Me.&#160; I am love, My children.&#160; I am truth.&#160; I am mercy.&#160; One day, your family members will understand and if they do not learn to love by the way you love them on earth, they will know later when they are either in purgatory or living in the joy of Heaven where all are completely understood, known and loved.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“Be at peace, even in trying circumstances for I am with you.&#160; Your time on earth is fleeting compared to your time in Heaven, so continue to love and serve.&#160; If you have not been one who loves, then go to Confession now and begin anew.&#160; Each soul on earth can begin anew and it is especially easy for souls who have access to the Sacraments.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;You make everything sound simple, Jesus, and it is simple, but not easy.&#160; Lord, it is very challenging for some, especially those in difficult situations in their families.&#160; But, I know You are completely aware of each person’s individual situation and You are with them, Lord.&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“Yes, My little lamb.&#160; Some have very difficult family lives or just one or two very challenging and hard to love family members.&#160; This message is especially for them.&#160; The more challenging the situation, the more meritorious and heroic the love.&#160; It is never easy to love those who do not love in return and yet it must be the way for all Christians.&#160; How will the world know love if My love is not given away for free?&#160; Love freely given, with joy for the sake of love is the way to penetrate hard heartedness, My children.&#160; Even pagans respond to unconditional love and kindness.&#160; This is living the Gospel.&#160; My children I am not speaking about remaining in the home of one who threatens your life or is harming your children.&#160; In these cases, it is not loving to remain in physically harmful environments.&#160; You must protect yourselves and your children from this type of evil.&#160; Still, you are to forgive and pray for those who have injured you while remaining in a safe place.&#160; I am referring to loving and showing love to family members who do not know Me or do not love Me.&#160; I am referring to family members who are occupied with the things of this world versus those of Heaven and salvation.&#160; You must be loving, patient and kind to all family members.&#160; The little souls in your care need to see love in their parents.&#160; They learn from watching you.&#160; What are you teaching them that they will take to their own families some day?&#160; Are you teaching them to leave you alone?&#160; Are you teaching them to constantly entertain themselves with video games and all forms of electronic media?&#160; I can assure you, when they are grown, they will have been taught well to leave you alone and to entertain themselves.&#160; They will have learned to be very self-centered and to neglect their parents and in turn their own children.&#160; My Children of Light, wake up and realize this is not the plan God has for families.&#160; Families are the domestic church.&#160; If you are not living this way, it is time now to change.&#160; Live simple, quiet, beautiful lives.&#160; Teach your children skills for living.&#160; If you do not know how to do this because you were not given these valuable skills, then you can learn.&#160; It is not too late.&#160; Grow something in a pot if needed.&#160; Teach your children to plant seeds and water and tend to them together.&#160; Do simple tasks with them.&#160; They will enjoy spending time with you and they will become your loving children.&#160; They will not neglect you when you are old, because they will love you as you have loved them.&#160; If you do not have children, there are many other ways you can help another child, perhaps in your parish or in your neighborhood.&#160; Ask one to do simple chores for you, perhaps to work in your yard or to carry something for you.&#160; Give them praise for this.&#160; Call their parents and thank them for having and raising such good children.&#160; In this way, you will encourage both the children and their parents.&#160; If you cannot do this, pray for them, smile when you see one another and be kind.&#160; You never know how much your smile means to someone, but I know children.&#160; I know the value of such seemingly small acts of kindness, and though you forget the number of people you have given your smile to, I know each one.&#160; Make the world in which you live, warmer, kinder, more loving and hearts will begin to open to Me, Jesus.&#160; Hearts will be drawn to you because of your love.&#160; This message is simple today, My children because it is needed.&#160; These are urgent times caused by the lack of love and the absence of peace in the hearts of My own Children of Light.&#160; Mine are blending into the culture, and instead of changing it, are becoming part of it.&#160; Mine are called to holiness, to be set apart because of your unconditional love and mercy.&#160; In this way, the holy stand out.&#160; Others notice your humility, your service, your love.&#160; I do not want you to hide from the world, but to show your light.&#160; To hide from others is to cover your light with a basket.&#160; This is not living the Gospel.&#160; Be love, be mercy, be light, be joy.&#160; Love each soul you meet and each one with whom you live.&#160; It is possible, My children because I will make it so.&#160; I will give you the grace you need.&#160; It is yours for the asking.&#160; I am generous, My children and there is enough for everyone.&#160; Ask Me and I will assist you to love. &#160;Give Me your hearts, My children.&#160; I will water your souls with graces each time you pray and each time you avail yourselves of the Sacraments.&#160; When you give love to your enemies, or to those who are difficult to love, My love will replenish yours.&#160; Come to Me in stillness in the silence of prayer and you will meet Me, your Jesus who loves.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“Be at peace. &#160;I, your Jesus, am with you.&#160; I love you and you are Mine.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Thank You, Lord.&#160; I love You and am grateful for Your beautiful words of love and wisdom.&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“And I love you, My child.&#160; Thank you for writing My words.&#160; I know your fingers are sore today and it is difficult to write.&#160; I thank you for your sacrifice and for the love you have for your brothers and sisters.&#160; My child, I am with you.&#160; Do not become disheartened by all that you must do.&#160; This is a difficult time.&#160; Allow Me to carry you.&#160; Allow (name withheld) My son to carry you.&#160; All will be well, My child.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Oh, Lord, thank you.&#160; It is good to be here with You, Lord.&#160; Thank You for Holy Mass and Communion and for the Feast of the Immaculate Conception yesterday.&#160; Lord, thank You for helping me with my studies, for giving me clarity regarding what I should do going forward.&#160; Thank You for Your direction, Lord.&#160; Praise You, Lord for Your kindness, mercy and love.&#160; You are love, Lord.&#160; You are mercy and truth.&#160; Jesus, I believe in the power of Your name.&#160; In Your name I pray for (name withheld) who is very ill.&#160; Help her, Jesus to believe.&#160; Help her, Jesus.&#160; Heal her, Lord and give her all the graces her soul needs.&#160; Jesus, I pray also for (name withheld).&#160; Heal her by Your holy name and by Your precious blood.&#160; She is so ill, Lord but if You just say the word, (names withheld) will be healed.&#160; Jesus, I need healing, also.&#160; Please give me a loving heart.&#160; Give me the graces to love heroically, Lord.&#160; I should be more loving by now, Jesus and yet I am still very flawed.&#160; Heal me, Lord.&#160; Help me to be more generous, more sacrificial in my love.&#160; Help me, Jesus not to complain.&#160; After all, I have many, many blessings and Your love, which I do not deserve but for which I am very grateful.&#160; Thank You, Lord.&#160; Please bring those who have wandered from the faith back home again.&#160; Bring those who are outside of the faith into Your family, Lord.&#160; May all people of good will be converted this Advent Jesus so we can properly receive You, the Lord God on Christmas morning.&#160; I love You, Jesus, my Savior, my Beloved.&#160; Make my heart a flame of pure love for thee.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“My child, My child, all of My children, prepare your hearts now.&#160; Prepare your hearts for My coming at Christmas time.&#160; Prepare your hearts just as the angels prepared the shepherds for Christmas Eve.&#160; They came singing Alleluia and Gloria, announcing My birth.&#160; The shepherds did not think that angels would appear to them, nor that they were of high esteem, so were not expecting to be the first adorers of God sent to earth.&#160; Yet, they had open hearts and stood in awe of the angels and of their proclamation.&#160; Their ‘Glorias’ filled the heavens with magnificent music so sweet was the sound of the coming of the Messiah and the words all good Jews longed to hear.&#160; So long had the Jews awaited their Messiah, yet the poor shepherds did not understand in their humility how they could witness such a magnificent scene.&#160; Still, realizing they were poor shepherds, with no gifts to bring, thought of My needs.&#160; They thought, as good parents, how uncomfortable I would be lying in a manger and so they brought soft, warm fleece to keep Me warm and to lie on in the manger.&#160; They brought milk for Me to drink until My Mother’s milk came in and they brought a lamb, a firstborn to give My parents.&#160; They were poor, but they brought the best of what they had.&#160; They brought loving humble hearts.&#160; The younger shepherds brought pure hearts and they all came to worship Me, the long-awaited Messiah.&#160; Imagine how amazed they were when they realized I had just been born and they were chosen to be the first to worship and adore Me.&#160; This was a message for all the world, then and now that I came for the lowly, the poor, the humble, not for the proud and haughty.&#160; Though, I love the rich and the poor, the rich have a more difficult time loving and accepting Me.&#160; Especially, the rich who are proud and conceited.&#160; They have a difficult time worshipping the true God because they have erected many false idols.&#160; The shepherds also gave My Blessed Mother and St. Joseph much respect.&#160; They asked what they could do to help when they realized the Son of God was born in such a poor state of circumstances.&#160; Mary and Joseph did not look down on the shepherds, as they had pure hearts and were filled with love.&#160; They marveled as the shepherds recounted the angels, the singing, the telling of My birth and where and how to find Me.&#160; What a sacred, holy night this was.&#160; How beautiful and pure My parents.&#160; There was much love, beauty and peace because of their deep love for God and their willingness to serve Me and do the Will of the Father.&#160; Oh, how beautiful are the humble souls who love God, who call Him Father, who adore Him, praise Him and glorify Him and yet who also call God friend.&#160; Remember, My children there can be deep joy in simplicity and in detachment from material things.&#160; The shepherds, as poor as they were, gave thoughtful, practical gifts.&#160; Even the Magi, with their gifts of gold and frankincense and myrrh gave practical gifts that were put to good use.&#160; Just as God the Father provided for Me, so shall He provide for each one of you in your need.&#160; He does so directly and also through others who love and serve Him.&#160; Take care of one another, My children and when you are generous, you imitate God, your Father who withholds nothing from you, even to the point of sharing His home with you one day when you are ready to come to Him.&#160; There is nothing needed in life that We withhold from you.&#160; You may wonder, then why there are those who are poor.&#160; This is only because the world does not love.&#160; There is enough for everyone, but many who have been made rich through the mercy of God refuse to share what they have with those in need.&#160; Do not ignore the plight of your brothers and sisters in need because you think they have not worked as hard as you or because you think they are less deserving.&#160; They may be more deserving than you, My children.&#160; You have the poor with you to teach you generosity.&#160; If you do not share, do not blame Me that they are poor.&#160; They are blessed spiritually and many of them will have a high place in Heaven because of their hearts.&#160; They help one another even though they have nothing.&#160; While you who have everything will help no one.&#160; Do you see, My children?&#160; The shepherds were poor, and yet they were chosen by God to see angels announcing My birth.&#160; They were chosen to see Me at My birth, to be the first to adore and worship Me.&#160; Besides Mary and St. Joseph, they were the first Christians, for they believed even before seeing Me.&#160; Out of their poverty, they brought gifts to comfort Me.&#160; I came for all peoples yet often only the poor truly love Me and open their hearts out of generosity.&#160; Be like the shepherds, My children.&#160; Do not be like the Pharisees who often condemned the poor.&#160; Be humble of heart and generous with your love and the gifts I give you. &#160;Remember, if I did not bless you with the means and the intellect, you would not have the material things you have.&#160; All good comes from God.&#160; Share with others and return the kindness of the Father by being merciful and generous with those who are less fortunate.&#160; Anyone in need of love, My children is poor.&#160; It isn’t just those living in poverty, but those who are lonely, those who are mourning the loss of loved ones, those who are ill, those who are lacking in love, who have hardened hearts.&#160; All these are in need of the love of God and they will find this love when you open your hearts and give My love away.&#160; Pray to know what it is I want you to do for the Kingdom, My children.&#160; First, allow Me to be born anew in your hearts.&#160; Welcome Me as the shepherds did.&#160; Adore Me.&#160; Honor Me.&#160; Then ask, as the shepherds did, ‘What can we do for our Messiah?&#160; What can we do to comfort Him and make Him know we love Him?’&#160; Ask this of yourselves, My Children of Light.&#160; Ask this of Me and My Holy Spirit will enlighten you.&#160; Then, in your humility ask Me to show you how to love others.&#160; Pray for them.&#160; Pray the Holy Rosary for peace in the world, and peace in the hearts of mankind.&#160; Pray, My children, but also act.&#160; You must put your love into action to be of service to others and in this way you show gratitude to the Lord your God who gives all that is good to His children.&#160; Open your hearts, My children so that when I come you will welcome Me and invite Me into your homes.&#160; I come to dwell with you in every Mass, but many refuse My graces, My dwelling.&#160; You are like one who opens the door, but does not invite Me in to stay.&#160; You turn your backs and walk away because you are unwilling to give Me a place to sleep and food to eat.&#160; You unite yourselves to Me in Holy Communion but leave Me standing in the cold with no blanket to keep Me warm, no food to eat and no one to love while you sleep in the warmth and comfort of the homes I provided for you.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;This is how you treat Me, your Savior who gave His life for you on the cross.&#160; This is how you treat Me when you judge your neighbor or look at the homeless in disgust.&#160; Remember, this is Me, My Children of Light.&#160; Love your neighbor who is standing on the corner with nothing but the clothes on their backs as you would love Me, for behold I am one with the poor.&#160; What you do to the least, you do to Me.&#160; Open your hearts, My children.&#160; Be transformed by My saving grace.&#160; Be filled with Sacramental graces and transform your lives.&#160; Live for Me, your Jesus as I live for you.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;Thank You, Jesus!&#160; Adoration Chapel&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h5&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Hello, Lord ever present in the Most Blessed Sacrament of the Altar.&#160; I love You, believe, hope and adore You, my Lord and my King.&#160; Jesus, thank You for all You do for me.&#160; Thank You for Holy Mass this morning and for Holy Communion.&#160; Thank You for my family, for my health and all blessings that come from You, Lord.&#160; Jesus, please forgive me of my sins.&#160; Help me, Jesus to love You more and more each day.&#160; Thank You for allowing me to meet the person and hear about (name withheld) for whom we have been praying for. (prayed for) Please resolve their situation, Lord in the way You Will for the best outcome for all of the souls involved.&#160; Praise You for healing (name withheld) and for the recovery of (name withheld).&#160; Jesus, You know all things.&#160; You know all who are physically, emotionally and spiritually ill.&#160; Please heal them all, Lord.&#160; Help our Church, Your Church in this summer of suffering.&#160; Purge our sinfulness, our pride, our haughtiness, our materialism and purify Your Church.&#160; Lord, I believe You that the gates of hell will not prevail against the Church, but there sure is a horrible battle raging.&#160; You, Lord will be victorious, but please spare those who have been wounded the most, the victims and the lives of their families.&#160; Heal them oh great Physician, my beautiful Jesus.&#160; Heal them and make them whole.&#160; Lord, bring all evil to light and purify us.&#160; Lord, a wound that is festering and full of infection must be lanced and drained.&#160; That is what I think You are doing with Your Church.&#160; You are splitting open the infected wound and draining the pus.&#160; Cleanse us, Jesus.&#160; Heal us, God our Savior, so that we can bring Your light to others, free of all infection.&#160; Jesus, there are places where gangrene has set in.&#160; In that case, physicians usually must amputate to save the limb.&#160; Lord, You are the only One who can heal something so severe.&#160; Please heal the limbs with gangrene, Jesus so they do not have to be cut off or separated forever.&#160; Save souls, Lord Jesus.&#160; Give miraculous graces for conversion, for repentance and for penance and sorrow in the hearts of those who have propagated these crimes and those who have hidden them so they could grow like cancer.&#160; Oh, Jesus You are the only One who can resolve this deep, dark, evil present in the Church and in the world.&#160; Come, Lord Jesus.&#160; Save us, Lord.&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Jesus, there are some who want to become priests, who feel called to discern a priestly vocation but who are fearful of being entrusted to strangers.&#160; They should be safe in the arms of Mother Church but because of betrayal do not know where to go or who can be trusted.&#160; Lord, give them courage and strength.&#160; Show them what they must do and where it is safe for them to go to answer Your call, Your invitation.&#160; Blessed Mother, Queen and Mother of the Church, help Your children and Your holy priest sons and those called by God to the priesthood.&#160; Now, more than ever, we need holy priests and religious.&#160; We need more vocations to the priesthood.&#160; Help us to be prepared for what is to come.&#160; Guide us and show us the way.&#160; Protect our sons, our grandsons Blessed Mother so they may be formed into the image of Your Priest Son, the High Priest, Your Jesus.&#160; Blessed Mother, gather us within Your holy mantle and protect us from evil. &#160;Help us to grow in holiness so that we, Your littlest children can stand with You and Jesus against evil.&#160; May our lives be pure and holy, Mother so that we will be also a sign of contradiction to the world.&#160; We, Blessed Mother, want to love as You love Jesus; we want to love as St. Joseph loves Jesus; we want to love as Jesus taught us to love, but we have so far to go on the road to love.&#160; I have far to go on this road, Blessed Mother.&#160; Take my hand and guide me.&#160; Take me in the footsteps of Jesus, so that with Your guidance, I will learn to walk the way of the cross, which is the way of love.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“My child, My child, My child, it is true what you say abut My Church.&#160; It has been true for some time.&#160; The wound has been festering until it can no longer remain hidden.&#160; Many lives have been shattered by this evil, but I can repair torn and shattered lives.&#160; Believe it, My little lamb for it is true.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Yes, Lord.&#160; I believe.&#160; I believe in You.&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“My daughter, you are also correct in thinking the worst is not over.&#160; Do not focus on this, though for it is My job to clean house.&#160; Just as I threw the money changers out of the synagogue so will I purge this evil from My Church.&#160; They have profaned the House of the Lord, My Church.&#160; They have desecrated My holy ones who are tabernacles of My Holy Spirit.&#160; They must repent.&#160; They must put on the sackcloth and ashes of repentance or truly I say to them, it would be better for them had they never been born.&#160; They have harmed My little ones, some were like My little St. John who loved Me in purity and truth.&#160; They have betrayed Me, these evil men who pose as My priest sons, like the Apostle Judas.&#160; They must repent of their evil ways, approach Me with contrition and beg for healing.&#160; I am all merciful and I will forgive even the worst sins, but I know all hearts.&#160; They must open their hearts to Me so that I can apply the fire of My love like a cauterizing iron.&#160; My child, My little one, do not cry.&#160; Your heart is crying out to Me.&#160; Do not fear.&#160; You have seldom felt My anguish and My wrath, little one.&#160; I know it seems fierce to you, My lamb.&#160; I am gentle now.&#160; Be at peace.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Jesus, You have every right to be our fierce Lion of Judah, for You are all holy and we are putrid sinners rotting from our spoiled hearts.&#160; Please save us, Jesus.&#160; Heal the wounds of all who have been victims and who have been robbed of their innocence and possibly from their love for You and Your Church.&#160; Oh, Jesus You are the One with righteous anger for You are God!&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“Yes, My child.&#160; You know Me as your gentle, adorable Jesus, and your understanding comforts and consoles Me.&#160; All who are sacrificing, doing penance and beseeching Heaven, I tell you; your prayers are not falling on deaf ears, for God hears all, sees all, knows all.&#160; Your prayers, your sacrifices have helped bring the putrid stench out of the dark and into the light.&#160; It has to be so, My faithful, little ones.&#160; Trust in your Jesus to do the purging and the purifying.&#160; I am also counting on you to do your part.&#160; Love one another.&#160; Pray and fast.&#160; Especially, pray the Holy Rosary and the Divine Mercy Chaplet given to you for just these times.&#160; Cleanse yourselves in the Sacrament of Reconciliation.&#160; Gather your families and pray together the prayer of the rosary and offer it for the healing of My little innocent ones and for My Church.&#160; Do not be afraid to speak out for the protection of the most vulnerable.&#160; This is the day for separating the goats from the lambs.&#160; Speak out in truth and also in great love.&#160; Be My witnesses.&#160; Bring mercy to those who are in need of mercy.&#160; Bring peace, the peace of Christ, your Jesus, to those who are in the world and do not know peace.&#160; Be love, be joy, My children.&#160; ‘How can we be joy now, Jesus with all that has been revealed?’ you may ask.&#160; You, My Children of Light know Me.&#160; You possess the Holy Spirit who dwells in the hearts of God’s children.&#160; You know and have learned the truths of the faith and of eternal life.&#160; Your inheritance awaits you, and so you can be joy.&#160; You must be joy.&#160; You must also have the peace that I give to you, especially now, My children.&#160; Especially now, for you are My disciples.&#160; You must continue to share My Gospel.&#160; The Church will survive, My little ones, for I have said so and I Will it.&#160; It has been planned before creation.&#160; The Father’s plan will come to fruition and you are living in these evil days because your lives are needed now, in this very time in history.&#160; Your lives, your souls, your love has been placed here at this time, to spread My love and to give My mercy in this time of great darkness.&#160; This is when the Children of Light will shine brighter than before because of the darkness in the hearts of mankind.&#160; You, Children of Light are the Church.&#160; Bring the downtrodden, the victimized, the lowly, the poor, the oppressed, the poor in spirit, into My Church.&#160; Welcome them.&#160; Teach them.&#160; Love them.&#160; It was no different in My days on earth.&#160; Those who accepted Me were the ones in need of a doctor and the ones who were looked down upon by society as well as the little children and those with pure hearts.&#160; They still exist today, My children and they are in need of their Savior.&#160; Go to them.&#160; Love them.&#160; Show them the way.&#160; Be love and mercy, peace and joy.&#160; I will give you every grace needed in these days.&#160; My Mother and Her little army, you, My children, will defeat satan with your love, your holiness, humility and purity.&#160; You must answer evil with holiness and humility.&#160; Look at My Mother and be humble, kind and meek as She was and is.&#160; She is the Holy Mother of the living God and She has nothing to do with evil.&#160; It has never touched Her.&#160; Be like Her, My children.&#160; Pray for this great grace, to become holy as My Mother is holy.&#160; She will guide you and teach you.&#160; She is the Mother of Grace.&#160; Do not be afraid.&#160; All of Heaven will assist you.&#160; I love you.&#160; Live holy lives and be pleasing to God the Eternal Father.&#160; All will be well.&#160; Trust in Me.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“My child, you may go now.&#160; Thank you for honoring My passion and My blood today, My child.*&#160;
