I love You.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“And I love you.&#160; Pray, My dearest little one.&#160; Pray.&#160; Be at peace and be love.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Amen, Jesus.&#160; I will do what I can with Your grace, Lord.&#160; Thank You, Jesus.&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;*Note: This is a reference to having prayed the precious blood prayers during Adoration that Jesus gave to Barnabus Nowye.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;wixGuard&quot;&gt;​&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;wixGuard&quot;&gt;​&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;h5 class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;span&gt;September 16, 2018&#160; Adoration Chapel&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h5&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Oh Lord Jesus Christ thank You for allowing us to visit You today in the Most Blessed Sacrament of the Altar.&#160; I adore You and praise You, my God and my King!&#160; I love You, my Jesus!&#160; Thank You for Holy Mass this morning.&#160; Thank You for Holy Communion.&#160; Lord, praise You for many answered prayers, especially for (name withheld) healing.&#160; Please be close in a special way to all who are ill.&#160; I pray for healing for (names withheld) and all who are on the church prayer list.&#160; I pray also for my friend (name withheld).&#160; Heal him, Lord Jesus.&#160; Jesus, please grant all that is needed for (name withheld).&#160; She is struggling, Lord.&#160; Be close to her and allow her to feel Your presence and a special closeness with Our Lady, Your Most Holy Mother Mary.&#160; Lord, I lay every burden and concern at the foot of Your most holy cross.&#160; Take each one and deal with them in the way only You can, My sweet Jesus.&#160; Lord Jesus, I trust in You.&#160; Jesus, I trust in You, Jesus, I trust in You.&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“My child, My child, your heart is heavy with concern for your child.&#160; She is My child, too little lamb.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Yes, Jesus.&#160; She was Yours first!&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“This is true little one and so I tell you I have a plan for My little, gentle one.&#160; She suffers so and I am aware of each suffering.&#160; She bears many crosses and I press each one to My suffering heart and lovingly hand each one to her.&#160; She bears them patiently, even the painful ones.&#160; We bear them together.&#160; She is not alone.&#160; Many souls from their triumphant place in Heaven intercede for her.&#160; They pray for her strength and fortitude to persevere in the trials.&#160; Her fidelity to the cross provides graces for many lost souls, even the soul of her friends in Purgatory who await their final purification.&#160; Your mother and grandmothers pray particularly hard for her.&#160; She is cherished by many in Heaven.&#160; She is cherished by the Holy Family.&#160; She is cherished by God the Father and God the Holy Spirit.&#160; All will be well.&#160; I have great plans for her, My little lamb.&#160; Tell her so.&#160; Encourage her.&#160; She is being guarded by My Saint Joan of Arc, her patron.&#160; My littlest one, think about your patron and all she accomplished on earth for Heaven.&#160; She was one small soul, but with My grace and through My Most Holy Mother, she went into battle, literally for France and for My Church.&#160; She was just a child really and yet it is the small ones God uses in a mighty way.&#160; You did not choose your patron St. Joan by chance.&#160; It was a mutual choosing, littlest one.&#160; She chose you, also.&#160; This should tell you something.&#160; Reflect on this.&#160; Pray to Me and I will give you insight.&#160; Ask for your patron saint’s intercession in the battles you face, My beloved child.&#160; You face these spiritual battles that are every bit as difficult as the physical battles.&#160; When you suffer, you are very, very close to My suffering, Sacred Heart.&#160; This is where you belong, My child, close to My heart.&#160; You have nothing to fear.&#160; You are where you belong and I will protect and care for you.&#160; Bring each care and each concern to Me, your Jesus.&#160; In this way, you must also release these burdens to Me.&#160; I am your friend and the only one who can solve each problem, therefore do not hold tight to that which you bring Me.&#160; You would not bring a gift to someone then hold tight to it while extending it to them.&#160; Would you, My little flower?&#160; Of course you wouldn’t.&#160; That would be ridiculous, would it not?&#160; My child, My generous one, when you bring someone a gift from your heart, you freely give it to them.&#160; There is joy in the giving.&#160; You must do this, also when you bring your concerns to Me.&#160; Release them to Me.&#160; Then do not worry.&#160; It is alright to think, ‘I wonder how Jesus is going to solve this problem.&#160; I wonder what beautiful result will follow.’&#160; You may think about this, My child and be open to how I may surprise you.&#160; When you give Me a problem, but continue to worry, fret and be sad, you are in essence saying, ‘I gave this to Jesus, but I don’t trust Him with my gift therefore I will hold on to it!’&#160; You see, My child, that is not really giving it to Me.&#160; That is not a way to trust your Jesus with that which you hold dear to you.&#160; My little one, I do not say this to scold you, only to teach you.&#160; I cannot do much with something which I have not been given.&#160; I need to have it completely and with trust.&#160; Then, I am at liberty to do My Will.&#160; Otherwise, out of respect for your will, I just continue to wait until you are ready to fully trust Me.&#160; The longer it takes, the more sad and troubled My little one becomes.&#160; This makes Me sad, also.&#160; What am I to do!&#160; I stand close by, listening, and loving you, but I am afraid I am not as much help as I could be.&#160; Give to Me completely, all that troubles you and then be joyful and await My work in each situation.&#160; You will see how quickly your Jesus can work when I am allowed to do so and trusted with the results.&#160; I can be trusted, I assure you for I have all the answers in the universe because—I am the answer. (smiling) Now, I want you to reflect on all I have told you and decide how we shall continue together in this great plan I have for your beautiful life.&#160; I love you.&#160; Let us begin.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Thank You, Jesus for Your deep love, Your tender affection, Lord and Your gentility.&#160; I love You, Lord.&#160; May everyone on earth realize how beautiful, how magnificent You are.&#160; Praise You, Jesus!&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“My child, My child, it is time for My children to realize how close the Time of Great Trials is and the chastisements that will be the climax of all chastisements thus far in history.&#160; Mankind must prepare.&#160; Go to the Sacrament of Reconciliation and be reconciled to God, His Church and to all of Heaven.&#160; Be close to Me in the Eucharist.&#160; Love one another and live the Gospel.&#160; Forgive those who persecute you and who turn against you.&#160; Forgive, forgive, forgive.&#160; Be concerned only for souls.&#160; Time is short now.&#160; Some will lose their lives.&#160; Pray that their souls will be ready for Heaven.&#160; Pray hard for those who do evil, and for those who do not know the love of God.&#160; In these days, conversion is more difficult for evil abounds and souls are easily tempted.&#160; In this day, more holy souls, prayer warriors are needed, but instead I have fewer souls praying.&#160; This means, those of you who are close to Me and who pray must pray more.&#160; It will be possible if you ask Me to show you how to pray more.&#160; Pray from the heart, My children.&#160; Be aware of My presence when you pray.&#160; My Mother is also present with you as are the angels and saints.&#160; Call on them often.&#160; They will assist you in your prayers.&#160; I need you, My children to send forth prayers to storm Heaven.&#160; The earth is very dark, indeed and your prayers are like rays of light in the darkness.&#160; They shine like spotlights and the rays reach Heaven.&#160; It is comforting to Me when you pray.&#160; My suffering heart was comforted on the cross because I saw you praying, though in the future.&#160; To Me all time is one and therefore the prayers you pray now, brought Me comfort then.&#160; I know this is difficult for you to understand, My Children of Light, but it is true.&#160; I saw you, I knew you before you were born and I knew all the holy acts of love you would do for love of your Jesus.&#160; Yes, I knew each sin, also and this is why I willingly died, so that you would be with Me one day in Heaven.&#160; I loved you this much, My children, to die for your sins, before you were even born, before you ever committed the first sin.&#160; See how deeply I love you?&#160; I do not hold your sins against you, My children as the evil one would have you think.&#160; If I did, would it not mean that My death was in vain?&#160; Do you see how false this notion is, My little children?&#160; I died for your sins to redeem you from them and therefore from death.&#160; Why would I hold your sins against you?&#160; Did I not say from the cross, to My Father in Heaven, ‘Father, forgive them for they know not what they do?’&#160; Yes, I prayed this prayer; not only for those who crucified Me and who wanted My crucifixion, but also for you.&#160; I understand weakness, My children.&#160; I understand temptation, even though I did not fall to temptation.&#160; Repent and return to Me, My little children of God.&#160; I am waiting with open arms for you.&#160; I am like the father of the prodigal son.&#160; I await you with open arms and I am ready for you to reconcile with Me.&#160; Go to Confession, My children to be cleansed of your sins and then come to the banquet I have prepared just for you.&#160; Partake of My body, blood, soul and divinity in Holy Communion with your Lord Jesus.&#160; This is the banquet I long for you to attend.&#160; Do not remain on the fringes as one who peers through the window watching the wedding party.&#160; Cleanse yourself in Confession and come to the banquet My children.&#160; I want you here with Me.&#160; I want to be one with you.&#160; I love you.&#160; Be at peace.&#160; Do as I ask, My children for I want what is best for you.&#160; I am what is best for you and I await you.&#160; The time is short.&#160; Do not procrastinate in receiving the God who loves you.”&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Thank You for Your love and mercy, Jesus.&#160; Forgive me of my sins, Lord.&#160; Help me to grow closer to You, My Jesus.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“My little lamb, offer your suffering, your work, your studies to Me.&#160; This is also a form of prayer.&#160; I know you long for more time to pray.&#160; I will help you.&#160; For now, each hour can be offered as a sacrifice for souls who do not desire prayer, who do not want to be close to Me.&#160; You are human and can only do as much as your body allows you, for you need to sleep, My child.&#160; I am giving you and My son (name withheld) many graces in this time of sacrifice.&#160; Use this time for Me, by offering this, too as a cross.&#160; I will use whatever you give to Me.&#160; Please try to be more joyful, for truly what you are doing is also a form of prayer and I can use it for the good of souls.&#160; I love you.&#160; You are Mine and I am yours.&#160; We are close friends, are we not? &#160;We are, My child, and close friends understand one another.&#160; There now, so you understand what I am saying and the meaning, My child.&#160; We are friends.&#160; We love one another regardless what life brings and we walk together.&#160; I am always with you.&#160; I will answer your payer about being more aware of My presence each day.&#160; This is a holy request, My child.&#160; It is good that you want to be with Me more and I want this also.&#160; Be of good cheer.&#160; This will soon be behind you and you will see that I gave you all that was needed, both of you, to get through this difficult time.&#160; Draw closer to one another.&#160; Pray together as I have asked.&#160; It is a time of unity with one another and with Me.&#160; Draw close to your family, also.&#160; Even if you are not physically together, be united as a family in prayer.&#160; Your family is much more important than you know.&#160; You will be very grateful to Me one day when you understand just how important each one is for souls and for Heaven.&#160; Believe this My children.&#160; (Name withheld), My son, treasure the lives of your children, your wife, for I brought you together for an important reason.&#160; Many reasons, really but you will understand one day just how precious each one is.&#160; You must see this now as the spiritual leader that you are for them.&#160; This is your domestic church and you are like a priest for your family.&#160; Love them.&#160; Protect them.&#160; Father them, My son.&#160; St. Joseph is assisting you and he will assist you even more when you ask him to do so.&#160; I bless you all now, in the name of My Father, in My name and in the name of My Holy Spirit.&#160; Go in My peace.&#160; Be joy to one another.&#160; Have light hearts so that My light will illuminate the darkness of the world as you go about your duties.&#160; I love you.&#160; I am with you.&#160; All will be well.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Amen, Jesus!&#160; Alleluia.&#160; Praise to the Holy Trinity!&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;"},{"id":9550,"datePublished":"2019-01-24T00:00:00","nodeName":"Recent Msgs Nov 4th-25th","pageTitle":"Recent Messages","subtitle":"November 4th - 25th","author":"","visionary":"Children of the Renewal","visionaryId":9538,"originalSource":"","originalSourceName":"","lstDateOfMsgs":["2019-11-04T00:00:00","2019-11-25T00:00:00"],"content":"&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;November 25, 2018, Feast of Christ the King, Adoration Chapel&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Hello, my adorable Jesus ever present in the Blessed Sacrament of the Altar.&#160; It is good to be here with You, Lord.&#160; Happy feast day, Jesus!&#160; Thank You for Holy Mass this morning!&#160; Thank You for Holy Communion.&#160; I am grateful for the blessings You give me, Lord.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Jesus, there are many people who are very ill.&#160; Please help (name withheld) who is extremely ill.&#160; Heal her, Jesus.&#160; I pray also for (names withheld) and all who are ill and on the church prayer list.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Lord, as Advent approaches, prepare my heart so that I am ready to welcome Your birth as if it was happening for the first time.&#160; Help me to have the faith of the shepherds, Jesus who left everything to find You.&#160; Lord, please guide me in all that I do this week and all that I need to do.&#160; Help me with my studies.&#160; Thank You for the help You have already provided.&#160; Thank You for being with (name withheld) during his test.&#160; We are so thankful, Lord.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Jesus, is there anything to say to me?&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“Yes, My child, all that I have told to My son (name withheld) is accurate.&#160; My patience is untiring and knows no bounds.&#160; My patience is divine.&#160; I await more souls in their conversion process, for I do not want even one soul to be lost.&#160; I love each person created as My sons and daughters.&#160; More souls would convert if more of My Children of Light extended love to them.&#160; My children, I need you to show My love to everyone you encounter.&#160; Be merciful and be peace.&#160; You will never run out of My peace, as long as you return to Me, the source of peace.&#160; Give all to others and return to Me.&#160; I will replenish you.&#160; I am the Prince of Peace.&#160; My children, look around you during this coming holy season and find people in need and then help them.&#160; There are homeless, there are children who are in families filled with conflict, there are elderly people who are unable to go out from their homes; there are countless situations people find themselves in and do not let anyone know.&#160; Befriend them.&#160; Ask what they need.&#160; Be kind and loving.&#160; Many just need your warm smile and conversation to know that someone cares, and notices them.&#160; Do not let each day pass, going about your busy-ness, too focused on your own problems to notice one standing in your midst.&#160; Acknowledge people.&#160; Speak with them.&#160; If you can help someone materially, do so.&#160; When you help one of your brothers and sisters you are being kind to Me.&#160; This is the way to store up heavenly treasures.&#160; It is also the path to My Kingdom.&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Thank You, Lord.&#160; How many times You have said these things to me and in spite of their simplicity, I do not do this every day.&#160; Help me to be more kind, Jesus and less focused on myself and all that I need to accomplish.&#160; Lord, please bless all who came into the church last evening.&#160; May they always be faithful Catholics.&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“I hear your prayers, My child.&#160; I accept them and hold them close to My Sacred Heart.&#160; Prepare, My little one as I have asked with prayers of the Rosary and Divine Mercy Chaplet.&#160; Pray with your families, the most Holy Rosary every evening.&#160; Bless them with holy water each night, and before they leave the house each day.&#160; I will give the children many graces in these days; graces of protection, peace, mercy and love.&#160; My children, and I am speaking now to the young ones, you are not only the future of the Church, but you are also important now.&#160; Your prayers, prayers of the innocent ones avail much from Heaven.&#160; If only you could see what occurs in the spiritual world, you would not find spiritual works to be ‘boring.’&#160; They are in fact far from being boring, but you must have faith for now and do what your Jesus asks of you, just because you love Me and I love you.&#160; I will fill all of My children with much grace when you are open to Me and when you seek Me.&#160; I am sending you out to change hearts, and in this way you will cooperate with Me to change the world.&#160; I am God.&#160; I am your Savior.&#160; I am the Redeemer of the entire world, and yet I need you.&#160; I need you because I love you.&#160; You need Me, also My children and therefore we must work together to usher in My Kingdom.&#160; My Kingdom must first come to the hearts of My people.&#160; Give Me your open hearts and I will fill you with My love.&#160; I will fill you with My mercy and My power over sin and evil.&#160; My Mother intercedes for you.&#160; All of Heaven prays for you and your success in following Me.&#160; Do not be afraid to love, be bold in your love, generous with your mercy.&#160; Bring each problem, challenge and obstacle to Me, My children.&#160; We will resolve each problem together.&#160; We are one, My friends, My children.&#160; I love you and I am preparing you with these lessons of love.&#160; I prepare you as I did My first disciples.&#160; You must be like the early disciples and rebuild My Church.&#160; The Church is being purified now and this purification will continue.&#160; Do not fear if you see the Church growing smaller.&#160; Do not fear the time of persecution that is surely coming.&#160; You will still spread My Gospel and there will be many miracles and conversions.&#160; You must open your hearts now to the love I am calling you to be so that you will be prepared for this time that is coming.&#160; You will be like rescue workers sent out into the pitch-black darkness, but the Holy Spirit dwelling within you will be like your helmet equipped with a head lamp.&#160; You will be My search and rescue squad sent out in the darkness to find lost souls in danger.&#160; If they are not found they will die from being exposed to the elements.&#160; Practice loving now, My children, for great acts of love will be required of you and you must learn now by doing the small acts of love.&#160; Do not begrudge others.&#160; Do not grumble and gripe but do everything out of joy and gratitude, for you know and love the Lord God who is your friend and you have everything when you have Me.&#160; No one can take Me from you.&#160; The more you give away to others out of love, the more you will receive from Me.&#160; Do not be afraid to give your love.&#160; Imitate your Jesus who withholds nothing from you.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Thank You, Jesus!&#160; I love You.&#160; Help me love You even more.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“My little lamb, thank you for being here with Me today.&#160; It is good to see you and My son (name withheld).&#160; Please pray as I have taught you and spend time with Me in the Holy Rosary.&#160; It is important to pray as a family.&#160; Put Me first in all you do and I will arrange things so that all will work out.&#160; I am the Creation of time.&#160; I love you.&#160; I bless you now in My Father’s name, in My name and in the name of My Holy Spirit.&#160; Go in peace and remember that where you go, I go with you.&#160; You are never alone, but I am there in your midst.&#160; Share My love with others who are desperately in need of My love.&#160; All will be well.&#160; Go out in My name.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Thank You, my Lord and my God, my Jesus of love and mercy.&#160; Praise You Christ the King of the Universe!&#160; Amen and Alleluia!&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;wixGuard&quot;&gt;​&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;hr /&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;November 11, 2018&#160; Adoration Chapel&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Hello, Jesus ever present in the Most Blessed Sacrament of the Altar.&#160; It is good to be here with You, my Lord and my God!&#160; Praise to You, Lord Jesus Christ.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Lord, please heal (name withheld).&#160; Help her, Jesus, she is so ill.&#160; I pray also for (names withheld) and for all who suffer including all who are on the church sick list and Cursillo prayer list.&#160; Lord, I pray also for those who have left the Church or are outside the Church (names withheld) as well as for those who do not know of Your love or have rejected Your love.&#160; For (names withheld).&#160; I also ask for Your healing for (name withheld).&#160; Thank You for Your grace and blessings for those You have healed in my family.&#160; Praise You, Lord!&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Lord, please open the hearts of those You are calling to the priesthood and religious life.&#160; Help them to hear and to say ‘yes’ to You.&#160; Bless all who will be at the Bishops’ Conference.&#160; Guide, guard and direct conversations, Lord so that all will be done in Your holy name.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“My child it is good that you and My son (name withheld) are here with Me today.&#160; These are pivotal times, My children.&#160; You do not understand this fully, but one day you will see in the Spirit.&#160; My little one, you understand, but not fully.&#160; Those who surround the shepherds of the Church are like the vipers in My days on earth.&#160; The Scribes and Pharisees who did not have love in their hearts, but only pride, jealousy and greed were the forerunners of those who surround the Magisterium today.&#160; They bite, sneer and plot in order to lead many souls astray.&#160; My child, I returned their contempt with love and concern for the state of their souls.&#160; I held out peace to them longing in My heart for their contrition, repentance and return to Me.&#160; There was genuine contempt for Me out of what they thought was blasphemy.&#160; I knew this and I had mercy.&#160; But through their rejection and anger, the seed of hatred grew until they were consumed with their evil plans to kill Me.&#160; My child, there was a possibility early on, for their souls, but instead of being open to the grace by seeing God’s Will, by asking for God’s guidance, they began to focus on evil, on their fears for what they would lose if the people of God followed Me.&#160; They were arrogant when they could have been humble.&#160; It was not My Will that they cooperate with evil.&#160; Yes, the Son of Man came to redeem and to save and that involved the cross, but these men did not have to cooperate with evil.&#160; Pagans would have done so, and I would have redeemed mankind regardless, but to have the children of Abraham, Isaac and Jacob betray Me was more painful.&#160; My child, you must realize that all throughout the history of the Church, beginning with one of My own, Judas, there have been people who want to destroy My Church.&#160; You must pray for these lost sheep and beg for their forgiveness.&#160; They were created in My image and likeness and they are children of God, also.&#160; Pray for them.&#160; They need your prayers.&#160; Ask the Holy Spirit to limit the influence and power they have over those less grounded in the faith.&#160; They confuse even the wise, but they are no match for the Holy Spirit, I assure you.&#160; There will be a cleansing of the Church first as there was of the temple in Jerusalem.&#160; If they refuse the graces being sent for their conversion, the Father will deal with them accordingly.&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;As for you, My Children of Light, be sure your hearts and souls are clean.&#160; Be pure yourselves.&#160; Forgive and pray for your enemies and for those who persecute and wound you.&#160; Then, you will be like your Savior.&#160; You will see what is in store for you in My Heavenly Kingdom because of your purity.&#160; So, focus on the work that needs to be done in your own souls.&#160; Do not judge.&#160; Do not look at those who are less fortunate and judge them.&#160; These poor in your midst, deserve love and peace.&#160; They deserve your mercy for they are My children, just as you are My children.&#160; Make peace and do not judge, but do what you can to assist them.&#160; In this way, you are loving Me, My children.&#160; Be love; be mercy; be peace; be joy.&#160; You cannot bring about conversion in wounded souls by being scornful, angry and judgmental.&#160; This only serves to wound them even more.&#160; You are called to be their fathers, brothers, sisters and mothers.&#160; You are called to love always and to show them the way to holiness.&#160; How can you show them My love when you put conditions on people?&#160; Love them exactly where they are; for then you will be like Me, your Savior.&#160; Be aware, My children that if you judge one of your brothers and sisters, it will not go well for you.&#160; I will not be able to use you to bring about My Kingdom when you act like the Pharisees and Scribes.&#160; Go now to seek the Sacraments and repent of your sins.&#160; The sin of pride blinds even those who are trying to follow Me.&#160; Pride is very deceptive.&#160; It lurks in the sin of self-righteousness, and in the sin of bigotry.&#160; Egoism is a symptom of prideful souls.&#160; You are not perfect either, My children and in some cases you are worse than those you judge.&#160; Do not judge the poor, either My children, even when you can see that their poor decisions brought about their circumstances.&#160; Who among you has made perfect decisions?&#160; Which of you has never made a mistake?&#160; You had the good fortune of having good upbringings or good friends to help steer you in the right direction.&#160; You do not know the woundedness of souls.&#160; Only I know what lies in the human heart.&#160; To think you know better is to put yourselves at the level of God.&#160; Do not commit this sin of pride, My children.&#160; Truly I tell you, you are to love those who are in need and care for them as you would care for Me.&#160; Change your foolish ways before it is too late.&#160; I placed your family members, your friends, your neighbors, and those you pass each day, in your lives for a reason.&#160; They are the opportunities for you to grow in holiness.&#160; Pray and reflect on this.&#160; Ask Me to show you where you need to change.&#160; I want only the best for you and the best is holiness.&#160; Do not fear that someone will take advantage of you.&#160; Everything you have comes from Me, My Children of Light.&#160; I can provide for your needs, but I am asking you to give to others in need and trust in Me to provide for you.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“The world has become very evil and still there are many souls who love Me and who are good.&#160; You must spread this goodness, My children.&#160; You must love, even when it does not make sense for this is what I do.&#160; I love you even though you were sinners and then you decided for Me.&#160; Give this same chance to others.&#160; Do not crush their souls because of your bitterness, your harshness.&#160; This is not being fatherly as you believe (falsely), it is condemning.&#160; Love as I have loved.&#160; Love as I love.&#160; Sacrifice as I sacrificed.&#160; Be merciful as I am merciful.&#160; This will be the cause of much healing, much love and much peace and you will see great conversions.&#160; Be patient with those I have given you to love.&#160; Each harsh word; each action made out of pridefulness will be noted, My children.&#160; I see all.&#160; I am everywhere.&#160; You cannot hide your actions from Me.&#160; Do everything in love and for love.&#160; My Spirit is with you and I will guide you.&#160; You must be gentle, humble and meek.&#160; My Spirit will work through you when you love.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“That is all, My little lamb.&#160; You are weary.&#160; Lean on Me and together we will walk towards the Kingdom.&#160; Lean on Me, My child.&#160; I will provide.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Yes, Jesus.&#160; Thank You, Lord.&#160; I love You.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“And I love you.&#160; I am with you.&#160; All will be well.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Amen!&#160; Alleluia!&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“I bless you in My Father’s name, in My name and in the name of My Holy Spirit.&#160; Be love to all, My child.&#160; Give others My love.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Yes, Jesus.&#160; If You help me I can.&#160; I love You and I will love others, with Your help and Your grace.&#160; Fill me, Lord for I am depleted.&#160; Give me Your heart, Lord and the heart of Your Mother so that I can love as You love.&#160; Thank You, Jesus, for Your words and for Your love.&#160; Amen!&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;wixGuard&quot;&gt;​&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;wixGuard&quot;&gt;​&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;hr /&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;November 4, 2018 Adoration Chapel&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Hello, Jesus present in the Most Blessed Sacrament of the Altar.&#160; I am glad to be here with You, Jesus!&#160; Thank You for Holy Mass and Communion this morning, and also for the beautiful choir concert after Mass.&#160; I’m grateful to You for the Ultreya last evening and for the testimonies of the candidates.&#160; Praise You, Lord that Your Holy Spirit is moving so visibly in these days.&#160; We need You, Lord.&#160; Please pour out Your Spirit and renew the face of the earth.&#160; Lord, thank You also that I was able to see (name withheld) after Mass.&#160; Her heart is breaking with grief, Jesus.&#160; Help her, Lord.&#160; Console her, Jesus and Blessed Mother.&#160; I pray for the repose of the soul of her father.&#160; Lord, please give us many graces during this election period and guide Your people to vote for pro-life candidates.&#160; We need Your grace, Lord to remove the blinders from our eyes and to see through Your eyes.&#160; Lord, thank You for (names withheld) and all those who are so faithful to come to adore You.&#160; Many are elderly, Jesus and they are very dedicated to You.&#160; Where would we be without their prayers and example.&#160; Lord, please be with all who are ill and all who do not know Your love.&#160; Manifest Your nearness and Your love to them.&#160; Help them to know You are near.&#160; Be with the Bishops as they begin the conference, Lord.&#160; Guide them by the light of Your Holy Spirit.&#160; Please bring all who are away from Your Church, home, Jesus especially (names withheld) as well as those who are outside the Church, (names withheld).&#160; Please bless the seminarians and protect them.&#160; Bring us more vocations, and more people who hear and answer Your invitation.&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“My child, see Me in the weak and the poor that I send you.&#160; I visit you in them.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Ok, Jesus.&#160; Lord, I don’t see the weak and the poor.&#160; Do You mean You will send, Jesus or have I missed these You are referring to, because I am too blind or preoccupied to see?&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“My child, I mean the ones I send to you.&#160; You see them, My little lamb.&#160; You do not see them as being weak or poor, though because you see beauty in them.&#160; You do not focus on what they are lacking.&#160; Just as you see (name withheld), My faithful one who is older in her years on earth.&#160; She is physically weak and she is poor due to her needs, but not material needs.&#160; She is poor in her loneliness.&#160; Your kindness lifts her spirit and helps her to know she is loved.&#160; You saw Me in the man you saw looking in the trash bins downtown.&#160; Your heart went out to him and though he left before you could speak to him, I took your prayers for him and gave him the graces you requested I bestow on him.&#160; My child, you do not even remember the many encounters with others you have, for they seem small and insignificant to you.&#160; I tell you they are not insignificant to Me.&#160; My child, I point this out to you so that you will be encouraged and realize that even though you do not remember, I remember, because when you are kind to these who are poor and weak, you are showing kindness to Me, your Jesus.&#160; I know you are thinking that others do much more than you.&#160; I am not calling you to be ‘others’.&#160; I am calling you to be you and to minister and show love right where you are, in each moment of the day, where you work, where you live, where you pray.&#160; I invite all of My children to be more aware of those around you in every situation of your lives, while you go about your daily tasks, plans and routines.&#160; There is a hurting world all around you, My children.&#160; I walked the earth and showed you what it is to love.&#160; I encountered people everywhere I went.&#160; You do, also.&#160; Your environments are your mission fields just as My geographic region was My mission field.&#160; Think of this, My Children of Light, I did not travel overseas to other continents.&#160; I sent My Apostles to do that.&#160; I did not board airplanes (though we did not have them) to travel thousands of miles for My mission.&#160; I went where My Father sent Me, in My homeland and in the surrounding regions.&#160; My time was brief but I covered much ground right where I lived and worked and the neighboring towns.&#160; My children, you do not need to go far to be My emissaries of love.&#160; You are My ambassadors and you take Me wherever you go.&#160; Do not be miserly and keep Me all to yourselves.&#160; Share the love you have for Me and the love I have for you, with all you meet.&#160; Perhaps someone who passes you in the aisle at the grocery store is in desperate need to be acknowledged.&#160; Your smile and look of love may be the difference between a glimmer of hope and despair.&#160; Perhaps your handshake is the only human touch they will have all week.&#160; My child, you are not passing strangers, you are passing your brothers and sisters. You are all part of the family of God.&#160; You will see them again one day in Heaven and each of you will remember the brief encounters you had on earth.&#160; Do not waste any encounter, for I oversee them all and each one is important in the Kingdom of God.&#160; Small acts of kindness, through love, are very powerful, My children.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;If these small acts are so powerful, Jesus I can’t imagine how powerful larger acts of kindness are.&#160; There are many who risk their lives each day for our safety, Jesus like the police, the firefighters, the military and countless others.&#160; They often live heroic lives and even lose their lives for complete strangers.&#160; The missionaries who leave their homelands, some of them forever, to spread the Good News of the Gospel.&#160; Jesus, it does make the small encounters seem less important.&#160; But, I understand that each and every life is important to You, Jesus.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“Yes, My child.&#160; You are correct there are people living heroically each day.&#160; They sacrifice much for their fellowman.&#160; This is extremely important and meritorious.&#160; What I want My children to see is that you, also have a mission field.&#160; It may seem less glamorous, less dangerous, but it is no less important.&#160; I am counting on you, My children.&#160; If you do not extend yourselves to those in your midst, who will?&#160; Many times, you are the only one I send who can make an impact at exactly the right time.&#160; You do not know what is in the hearts of others, but I do.&#160; I know exactly what others need and the timing of your paths crossing is Providential (smiling).&#160; Please be more aware of your brothers and sisters, Children of Light.&#160; You have My light.&#160; You are to bring it to others.&#160; All others.&#160; Your roles are very important to the Kingdom of Heaven.&#160; You are not perfect, I know for I made you.&#160; My Apostles were not perfect, either.&#160; Some were not even as holy as My Children of Light in these days.&#160; Not at first, that is.&#160; They grew to magnificent holiness and love, but they were not at that level when they began to follow Me.&#160; Please do not underestimate what I can do working in and through you.&#160; You cannot do this mission alone, it is true.&#160; But oh, what we can do together!&#160; We will build the Kingdom of Heaven, My children.&#160; It is the Father’s Will.&#160; It is My Will.&#160; You must desire this, also.&#160; Pray for the grace to desire My Kingdom.&#160; Pray for the grace to work to bring it about.&#160; Pray for the graces to love heroically, and then be open to the graces I give to you.&#160; Be not afraid to love.&#160; There is nothing to fear.&#160; Be love, be mercy, be joy, be peace.&#160; I am with you.&#160; I give you My love, My mercy, My joy, My peace.&#160; You give it to others.&#160; Do not judge the lives others are living, for you do not know their circumstances.&#160; I do.&#160; You do not know the depth of their wounds.&#160; I do.&#160; You do not know how they have been treated, and if they were raised with no love in their lives.&#160; I do.&#160; You do not know how many times they were abused by those who were supposed to care for them and protect them.&#160; I do.&#160; You do not know anything about their souls, My children.&#160; I do.&#160; Therefore, you are not to judge them or criticize them.&#160; Only love them and show them love.&#160; Some will tell you they do not deserve your love.&#160; You will spoil them, or they will get the wrong idea that it’s alright to be the way they are!&#160; My children, this is nonsense.&#160; Do I not spoil all of My children by providing sunshine to nourish the plants you need to eat and to make the flowers and trees grow?&#160; Do I not provide the rain to keep you from having a draught?&#160; Do I not provide a nice breeze on a hot summer day to cool you?&#160; Do I not provide the birds, the fish, the animals and the plant life for you?&#160; Which one of you is so godly that you have never sinned?&#160; Which of you deserves every good thing you have?&#160; Did I not give you talents, intelligence and skills to earn a living?&#160; Yes, you cooperate with My gifts by working, but which of you endowed yourselves with these gifts at birth?&#160; None of you, My children.&#160; You know the answers to these questions because they are obvious to you now, but how often do you reflect on these things?&#160; Many are quick to judge those who struggle in life, but fail to see that only by My grace are your lives different.&#160; My children, it is part of My plan to give some more material gifts than others, because you need to be made holy through the sharing of your gifts with others who cannot repay you.&#160; Do you see, My children?&#160; Many of My children who are living in poverty are holy.&#160; They do not like the lives they have, and yet many accept their crosses with humility.&#160; It is difficult to ask others for help.&#160; Do not look down on those who need your help.&#160; One day, everyone needs help, My children.&#160; When you are elderly or infirmed, you will also need help.&#160; It is part of the human condition.&#160; Be generous with your assistance, your kindness, your good deeds.&#160; Begin first with your own families for these are often the most important mission fields.&#160; Do not ignore others, though but go outside your ‘inner circles’ and be kind and merciful to others.&#160; My children, your Jesus did not have to speak to your parents and grandparents in this way, for they read Scripture and they knew how to help one another.&#160; It was part of their way of life.&#160; Neighbors helped neighbors and anyone who crossed their paths in need.&#160; Even if there wasn’t as much financial prosperity, there was generosity and hospitality.&#160; My children of this age are losing the art of hospitality and generosity.&#160; Be more aware of those in need.&#160; Some are not poor materially, but are lonely, grieving or have too much stress and strain in their lives.&#160; Perhaps they are caring for loved ones who are ill and they are working and raising a family.&#160; What can you do for them?&#160; Perhaps cook a meal, or visit with their sick family member, or run errands for them.&#160; Pray for them, speak with them.&#160; Let them know that you care and that you notice.&#160; You may be the only one who extends this kindness.&#160; The world will be a better place, My children for your love. You must learn to live in this way of love now, or you will not be prepared for the life of love in Heaven. &#160;Heaven is all love, My children.&#160; It is being in the presence of Love Himself.&#160; It is the fullness of love.&#160; You must begin to live as if you were living in Heaven now.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Thank You, Lord Jesus for reminding me how important each day that You give us is, in bringing about Your Kingdom.&#160; Thank You for making it easy to understand and simple, Jesus.&#160; Thank You for each encounter You give us with others.&#160; Help me to see each person as a blessing and a gift from You, Lord.&#160; Thank You for the many times You have sent people to help me.&#160; Each smile and hug given to Me was really a gift from You and I am very grateful.&#160; Thank You for Your beautiful, unconditional love, Jesus.&#160; Thank You for Your infinite mercy, Your forgiveness, Your peace.&#160; Jesus, You know each and every concern on my heart.&#160; Take these concerns, Lord and deal with them as You see fit.&#160; Help me with the heart condition I have, Lord.&#160; I offer it for all who have broken hearts, who do not know love or the source of love.&#160; Help my children and grandchildren to love and follow You, Lord.&#160; See to each one’s needs and give them what they need for their souls and hearts.&#160; Thank You, Jesus that You hold each person in the palm of Your hand.&#160; Praise You and thank You, my Lord and my God.&#160; I love!&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;“And I love you, My child.&#160; I take your sufferings and your offerings in prayer, and I will use them for the good of the Kingdom.&#160; Thank You, My little lamb for your love and your friendship.&#160; You may go now in peace, My child.&#160; I am with you.&#160; I bless you and My son (name withheld) in the name of My Father, in My name and in the name of My Holy Spirit.&#160; Be mercy, be love, be peace, be joy.&#160; I will provide all that is needed.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;&#160;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p class=&quot;font_8&quot;&gt;Thank You, my Jesus.&#160; Amen!&#160; Alleluia!&lt;/p&gt;"},{"id":9501,"datePublished":"2019-01-07T00:00:00","nodeName":"Recent Messages to  Children of the Renewal Messages","pageTitle":"Recent Messages to  Children of the Renewal Messages","subtitle":"September - October, 2018","author":"","visionary":"Children of the Renewal","visionaryId":9538,"originalSource":"","originalSourceName":"","lstDateOfMsgs":[],"content":"&lt;p&gt;October 28, 2018 Adoration Chapel&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;Hello, my Jesus ever present in the Most Blessed Sacrament of the Altar. I believe in You, love You and adore You, my God and my King. Lord, it is good to be here with You. Thank You for Holy Mass this morning and for Holy Communion. Thank You for (names withheld). Thank You for allowing us to be together at Mass. Jesus, bless (names withheld) who were not there. Please bring (name withheld) back to the Church as well as (names withheld). Please bring (names withheld) into the Church. Lord, thank You for our pastor (name withheld) and for (name withheld). Thank You for protecting (name withheld) during his car accident. Praise You that he wasn’t hurt. Thank You, Jesus for our family party yesterday for (name withheld). Help our entire family to grow closer to You, Lord. Jesus, please comfort (name withheld). Her heart is grieving her Father’s death and not being able to be by his side makes everything even worse. Help her mother to leave (location withheld) and come to be with (name withheld).&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;Please help the people of Venezuela, Lord to rebuild their economy. Their country has been decimated by their President and his party. Help them, Jesus to regain their freedom and to live lives of holiness, love and joy. Jesus, I trust in You. Jesus, I trust in You. Jesus, I trust in You. Lord, please help all Catholics to evangelize and spread the Gospel so that others will come to know You, love You and believe that You are Son of the Living God, true God and true man. Please grant graces to those You are calling into the priesthood and religious life. Help all to say ‘yes’ to Your invitation. Jesus, we need more priests in our diocese and in all dioceses in the world. Please send us an associate pastor, Jesus. We need more holy priests, Lord. Please see to it, Jesus. Lord, heal the sick, all those on the church prayer list and (names withheld) and all who are ill. Help (name withheld), Lord. He is so stressed now. Help him, Jesus.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;“My child, I know you are very tired and weary. I know and I am with you. Thank you for going to the memorial Mass to comfort (name withheld). Her heart is breaking, but My Mother comforts her.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;Thank You, Lord. Her earthly mother is so far away and (name withheld) is in a foreign land, though it is now her home. I’m sure she feels lost without her father and lost without her homeland. She must feel as if her world is chipping away, in a sense, and yet perhaps she will begin to feel that her true home is more and more close to her. (Heaven)&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;“My child, this is a painful part of life, having loved ones die and leave Earth for Heaven. It is more painful when one is unsure about a loved one’s soul and the disposition of it at death. Many people grieve more deeply for this reason. It is truly a gift when a loved one who is close to Me passes from this world and is born into Heaven. Even if souls who are close to Me need some purifying in Purgatory, their family can have confidence they will one day be in Heaven. It is not so for those who die outside of the family of God, because of their rejection of Me. But since you do not know for sure, it is a work of mercy to have Masses said for your loved ones and friends who have died and especially helpful for those in the process of dying for the graces of the Mass, applied to their souls before death can bring the gift of conversion. Do not withhold a Mass for souls in need, either in the act of dying or afterwards. Pray for souls in Purgatory, My child.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;Yes, Jesus.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;“My little lamb, keep your children and grandchildren safe by placing them under My Mother’s mantle of protection. Pray the prayer I gave to you, for all of your children and grandchildren. This is a powerful prayer for it is a request that My Sacred Heart and My Mother’s Immaculate Heart be the refuge of souls. Be confident in the protection of My Mother and in My protection. Even if some physical harm comes to those in My protection, be confident that we protect souls and this is the most important kind of protection. Be confident and trust, My Children of Light.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;Yes, Lord. Thank You, Jesus! Lord, please fulfill Your words regarding the matter of the community that will be discussed next week. Bring about Your Will in this matter, Lord. Restore what is due to people, but most of all, Lord, restore peace and love between all. Lord, we have no one to represent us but You. Therefore, we have the best! Father God, bring all to pass as You Will and as You said would be. Make it so, Father for You said You would. All for Your honor and glory, because no man can work out these impossible problems, but You can, Father. You are the God of the impossible, for nothing is impossible for You.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;“My child, no matter the outcome, trust in Me. I am the lover of your soul and I do what is best. In this, rest your confidence and your trust. Be at peace. I am God. All belongs to Me. I am the alpha and the omega, the beginning and the end and all that exists, does so by My Will and through My Will. You are My child, the children of God have the richness of Heaven for their inheritance. Nothing on earth, that is earthly wealth, material goods, are really lost if you have the Kingdom in your heart. Remember that where your heart is, there is your kingdom. All will be well, My child. Live out of this knowledge and count on it, for by counting on Me, your soul will have peace and joy.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;Thank You, Father. I love You. I praise You and You are my peace and joy. Give me a pure heart, Lord. Give me a heart for You and only You and Your Will.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;“This is a holy prayer, My child. You are growing in this purity and love for Me. Continue this pursuit, My little lamb.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;Yes, Lord. There is joy even in the pursuit. You make life exciting, Lord, even in spite of the crosses, the trials, the suffering. There is much joy because of You. Thank You for Your love, Your mercy and for the life of faith You give so freely to all who seek You.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;“My child, draw closer to the heart of My Son in Holy Mass and in Adoration. All who are close to My Son in the Eucharist, console His Sacred Heart, You are sealed in My love in this way.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;Thank You, my Lord and my God. I love You. All praise, honor and glory to You now and forever.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;Thank You, My little child. You may rest in My peace.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;Alleluia! Jesus, please protect our priests. Keep them safe and give them graces for holiness. Help us to “minister” to them, Lord as we want to serve others as You served others. Keep them safe, especially with all that will come to pass. Please protect our President and Vice President, their families and all cabinet members. Please help us in the fight to end all violence, especially abortion and euthanasia. Oh, Lord we are so miserable without You. We become worse than animals. Bring about conversion and the triumph of Your Mother’s Immaculate Heart.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;“My child, what you spoke about last evening regarding a reprieve is true. Things seem good in your country at the moment, but to remain this way will require the hard work of prayer, fasting, penance and more prayer. Do not become complacent, My Children of Light. Souls are on the precipice. They are hanging in the balance. Much, much prayer is needed. If there is an outpouring of prayer, especially the prayer of Scripture which is the Rosary, many souls will be converted and will be saved. If you all become (and in some cases, remain) complacent, souls will be lost and the reprieve will have been wasted. Do not waste this time, My children for this is not something to be taken for granted, but is a great blessing to My people who pleaded with Me to intervene. I intervened, My children, but you must do the same. Now, you must heighten your prayers and do so with a sense of urgency for it is then that you pray from the heart. Do not be lukewarm, My children. There is no time to waste. Be vigilant and remain actively in prayer. May your lives be a prayer and each activity an act of service and love for God and for your neighbor. You may go, My child and be always in My peace. I bless you in the name of My Father, in My name and in the name of My Holy Spirit. Go in My love. Be peace, be mercy and be joy, My child.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;Amen, Jesus. Alleluia!&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;​&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;October 21, 2018 Adoration Chapel&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;Hello my Jesus present in the Most Blessed Sacrament of the Altar. Give them every grace needed, Lord to carry out Your Will and mission. Thank You for my beautiful family, for my loving friends and for my husband who is so dear to me. Thank You for Your love, which is the best gift of all.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;Lord, please heal the sick, the wounded and bring them Your peace. Jesus, I trust in You. Jesus, I trust in You!&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;“My child, thank you for your words of trust. It is good that you trust in Me and trust in My mercy. It is very important in this age to spread the message of My mercy and My love. There are many, many souls who do not know or do not believe in My mercy. Tell people about My mercy and the messages I gave to My holy little Faustina. I want the world to know and so many do not. The world is in dire need of My mercy. You are wondering how you, who are little, can do this, My child, but it begins with you. It begins with each of My Children of Light. You be mercy and love to others. Speak of My mercy when you converse with others. Speak of the mercy of God and tell people there is no bottom to the well of My mercy. There is mercy for all, enough for every person ever born, living now, and for all who will be born. It is unendless and it is for everyone. Anyone who repents and appeals to My mercy will be saved. Come to Me, all who are in need of My mercy, and mercy shall be yours. The world is in severe darkness and many souls are deprived of light. I am the light. I will restore each and every soul who comes to Me. Do not wait until it is too late. Avail yourselves of My mercy now before you stand before Me as the just judge. My mercy is for all the living. No matter, how much evil you have done in your lives, it is not too late while you live on this earth. Once you pass from this life, your choice will have already been made. This is why My lost children, you must choose for Me now. There is much good we will do together, but first you must turn your back on your sins and walk toward Me, the light, the lover of your soul. I redeemed you at a great price, all for the love of your soul. Do not waste My love, but accept it and draw close to Me. Then, you will know peace. Now you know chaos, confusion and unrest. With Me, you will know order, clarity, peace and calm. You will feel really, truly alive, just as in your youth. Trust in My mercy. All will be well, but let us begin right away.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;“My child, you are thinking that because many know of St. Faustina’s diary that you do not need to be the ‘mouthpiece’ of My mercy beyond your daily encounters. This would be true, My child if the world really did know, but sadly they do not. Some are aware, yes. But many are still ignorant of the Gospel. You and all of My Children of Light must be My spokesperson. Live mercy, yes. This is of the utmost importance. But, I ask that you and all who follow Me, speak of My mercy. Be like the few loaves of bread and the fish that I multiplied. I do not need large crowds of people to make My message heard and spread. I need the few willing to be used and multiplied. But, I need each one of you. Do not turn away from this request, My Children of Light. This is a gift I give you, to be apostles of My mercy. If you do not know how to begin, ask Me to guide You. I am guiding and directing My children as in the days of the early Church. Yes, My little lamb, you heard Me correctly. I am pouring out My Spirit in powerful ways to bring many souls into the family of God. All that is needed are open and willing hearts. I will pour out gifts of My Spirit to give each one what is needed for the unique mission of each and every soul. Ask and pray for My Spirit to be given in new and powerful ways to bring about My Kingdom. You must be gifted for this work if you are to truly serve Me, My children for you are among the wolves. My protection is needed not only for your well being and security, but so that you can move out in the world among the wolves and bring My mercy, healing and love to those living in darkness. Yes, My children it is like the days of the early newborn Church. Consider that most people living in your times do not know God, do not love God, and do not believe in God. Consider that it is your mission to spread the Gospel to the ends of the earth. What will you do? Will you be like My first disciples and spread the message of love? Or, will you be like those who turned and walked away, too uncomfortable at the living Bread from Heaven? My Children of Light, you feel you have already chosen Me and you have but from this day forward now, you must make another choice, to share My love with the world in darkness. Do not say, ‘My family knows God, and my friends do also. We are fine and we will stick to ourselves.’ This is not love, My children. Did I not tell you in Holy Scripture that it is not enough to love your friends? Even the pagans do that. You must love your enemies. Love your enemies. Think of this. Who are your enemies? Are they not those who do not believe? Are they not those who are filled with anger and hate? Are they not those who have faith in pagan, false gods? I ask each one of you, ‘Who are your enemies?’ Visualize them, My little ones. Picture them in your mind. Then, see that I am standing near them also. I am concerned for these lost and confused souls. I died for them, also. They may be difficult now, but you should see what I see. I see how on fire with My love they could be. I see their hearts full of sorrow for their sins. I see the love they could have in their hearts, the many others they could impact if they knew Me. I see their wounds, their pain, the people in their lives who hurt them, often seriously wounded them. I see who they once were when they were little children, before they knew the corruption of sin and evil. I see them this way, My Children of Light, if you show them My love. If you pray and sacrifice for them. If you show them My mercy. If you give them My love. Yes, My little, brave souls. Their salvation depends on My act on Calvary, but it is to you I rely upon to tell them for they do not know. You are those I am calling. It is on you I rely. Think about it, please. Who else is there to send?”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;Oh, Jesus I hadn’t really thought about it this way. Of course, You are relying on us. Thank You, that You are. You could do all of this Yourself, but You never planned it that way. There are beautiful movements of My Spirit within the Church. It is time to take this Spirit of Mine out to more and more for the good of souls.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;“The New Springtime will come, My child, but there is work to do first. My little lamb, it is wintertime in the history of man. You know when winter is upon you that spring will come. However, when it snows, people must still plow the snow. You put out bird seed during the stark winter to feed My little birds. You wear heavy coats to keep warm and cover your beds with more blankets. You do all of this even though you know spring is coming for you cannot sit around idle until then. Neither can My children remain idle in spreading Christianity during this winter time of souls. You must show others the path of life, the path of truth and of love. You must prepare the way by your loving acts of kindness. You must give teaching and direction, just as in times of weather emergencies. It is no different in the spiritual world. Look around you and see the great need, My children. It is time to act for Me and for My Kingdom. It is time to act for love of neighbor. Make those who are enemies into friends by bringing them to the light. Awaken from your sleep and see there is much work to do for your Jesus. Remember, you are not alone. I am with you. Together, we will save souls. Let us begin, My Children of Light. Ask Me to show you what it is you can do. Pray for direction and it will be yours. Do not be inactive in this great time of need. Ask Me for graces and graces will be yours. Frequent the Sacraments and you will receive all that you need. I am relying upon you, My children. Souls are waiting to hear this Good News that is Jesus. Thank you, My little lamb for giving Me your will. Do not listen to the lies of the enemy who wants to condemn you. You belong to Me and I to you. No harm can come to your soul. Rejoice and be full of joy because I love you. This is true of all of My children. I love you!”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;Thank You, Jesus. Praise You, Lord. There are few places young people can be educated these days and be free from brainwashing. Lord, God help us. Save us from ourselves, Jesus. Rescue us, Lord. Our shepherds are either part of the problem or are afraid or too timid to speak out. The ones who do speak out have little authority to affect change. Jesus, what are we to do besides pray and fast? Please protect Your holy priest sons and religious. Thank You for those shepherds who are still faithful to You and to Your people.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;“My child, My child, did I not tell you it would be this way? They pay Me lip service, and think about living for Me, but proceed with their lives of entertainment and pursuit of material things. They do not live the Gospel message. They do not live as followers of Christ. They blend in to the world and the culture so much so that the world cannot see that they are Christians. Seek My face and be filled with My peace and My mercy. Your job is to love and follow Me. I will work through you where you are; wherever you are just as I put your family in the right place and time yesterday to assist another brother. Walk in My light, My little lamb. Do you not see My hand in all things? Yes, I know that you do, but I remind you of this. I know every hair on your head. I know exactly where you are at all times, for I go with you. I know this about each and every one of My children. There is no hiding from Me.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;“To My children living in evil, listen well. There is very little time for you. Blessed Mother, Queen and Mother of the Church raise holy young people to lead our Church. Teach us, good and holy Mother. Those who have love in their hearts and try to live holy lives will know and hear My Son’s voice. He is always guiding and directing, for He is the Good Shepherd who lays down His life for His sheep. It is only a matter of being in a state of grace to recognize His voice. Do not despair, nor be discouraged, but instead trust. God will provide an answer to every difficulty. What is needed is trust. Praise God for all He is and for all He has done for humanity. He is to be praised, in every circumstance. When you praise Him, you join your praises to those of the angels and saints. You become united with the inhabitants of Heaven who are your brothers and sisters. Be people of hope for your hope is in God. Keep your eyes on Heaven, My child. Heaven must be in your line of sight at all times. That is the way to deal with reality, by focusing on the reality of Heaven. Thy Kingdom come, thy will be done, on Earth as it is in Heaven. Let My Son’s words always be in your heart and on your lips. These words will be a consolation to you as well as a plea to the Father. These are God the Son’s words and they hold power, the power and love of My Son. My child, I am the Mother of the Church, for My Son put me in this place, and I intercede for His Church. Yet, mankind’s repentance and return to holiness will bring about the renewal that Holy St. Pope John Paul II, My son spoke of many years ago. My Immaculate Heart will triumph. For now, you and My other little ones are called to pray and make sacrifices of penance for the many sins that offend God. I will bless you with My Motherly blessing and send graces to you for love, holiness, and courage. I will protect My children under my Motherly Mantle so do not fear. Your Mother is beside you. Another, like the one you love, will be raised to lead the Church. My Son Wills it. Be love, and be like My Son.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;Thank You, Blessed Mother. You are in the midst of a great battle for souls and you must be My Soldiers of Light. You are in My Holy Mother Mary’s army. I remind you during this month of the Most Holy Rosary to pray as never before for My Church, for souls and for the coming of the Holy Spirit. I ask for a great tsunami of prayer now, at this time. My children, the Will of God is that you will become holy and pure now, in this current age and now while you are alive. Since there are many souls in peril and there is much darkness on account of sin, you are being called to the front lines to be defenders of the faith, teachers, servants and friends to those in darkness and in the shadows of death itself. Through prayer, sacrifices, fasting and frequenting the Sacraments, I will anoint you with special graces for these days. You are marked by My Seal. You are called to be My disciples. It is for this reason, due to My love, that you have been baptized into My Holy Catholic and Apostolic Church, the one true Church, so that by your life your witness, your service, you will rescue souls. I am counting on you, My Children of Light, to bear My Light, My love, My peace to a world in darkness. I will help you, My children, but you must be willing to accept My call, My invitation. Give me your ‘yes’ dearest children. I have no others to count on, no others waiting in the wings, so to speak. It is to you, I look with anticipation. Will you accept? Examine your hearts, My little ones. What is holding you back? Does something separate you from Me? What is in your life, or in your heart creating an obstacle to My Will. Let us examine this, and remove it at once, so that you are free to join My Mother’s army to usher in the Era of Peace, the New Springtime. Do not be afraid for I am gentle and merciful. I will give you every grace for this mission. So much so, that it will not seem to be as difficult as you may think it will be. Come, My children. Be confident in My love for you. Trust in Me and you will not be disappointed. Decide for God’s Will, My Children of Light. There is no time now, no room for those who are lukewarm to remain so. You are either for Me or against Me.”&lt;/p&gt;\r\n&lt;p&gt;Jesus, I love You and I want to do Your Will. Help me, Lord each and every moment to live within Your Will.
